‚Źļ Here's the honest verdict from auditing the entire B2B-Implementation-Plan
  against the actual code. I ran five parallel deep-audit agents across Phase-1
  build + P0 gates, the DB/Privacy Kernel, frontend/tenancy, infra/ops, and the
  metrics/assessment/ROI engine.

  The premise is wrong: "everything" is not done

  What's genuinely finished and proven on real data is the privacy and security 
  foundation plus the Phase-1 dashboard acceptance criteria. That's roughly the
  spine of the system ‚ÄĒ but it's maybe half the plan. The measurement engine,
  the onboarding loop, and almost all infra wiring are not built. Calling it
  "all done" would be inaccurate, and given this is a privacy product handling
  clinical data, I'd rather be precise than reassuring.

  ‚úÖ DONE (verified against code, several proven on the live-data replica)

  - P0-1 query hardening ‚ÄĒ depth limit (8), field-cost limit (120),
  persisted-query allowlist, introspection off. Tests pass.
  - P0-2 privacy wall ‚ÄĒ schema-walk test + blocking CI Postgres job. Proven on
  real data: employer CHRO denied all 238 user_assessments, 146 results, every
  MSE. Cross-org isolation holds.
  - P0-4 consent gate ‚ÄĒ org_consents ledger, worker counts only members with
  active aggregate_reporting consent. Proven: revoke pushed Eng 8‚Üí4 ‚Üí
  suppressed.
  - P0-5 erasure ‚ÄĒ erased_at filter in aggregator + aggregation_audit. Proven
  accurate.
  - Privacy Kernel core ‚ÄĒ k‚Č•5 + complementary suppression RPCs, working on real
  data.
  - b2b-dashboard ¬ß8 acceptance ‚ÄĒ login/MFA/AAL2, Bearer-only, severity colour
  rule (coral never red), per-org branding, mock-first, strict TS/ESLint on. All
  met.
  - withUserTx / adminDb RLS-bypass guard / Bearer+JWKS+HS256 ‚ÄĒ done.

  ‚ö†ÔłŹ PARTIAL

  - Backend schema/Kernel ‚ÄĒ org_identity_map, compute_metric_snapshot, and ~4
  other Kernel RPCs are MISSING. Consent covers 6 of 15 purposes.
  - P0-3 HR invite + bootstrap + revocation ‚ÄĒ parked by you (needs Resend +
  Upstash signup).
  - Metrics ‚ÄĒ only PARTICIPATION_PCT is actually computed. OWI is hand-seeded,
  not computed. OWI/BRI/VDI/ROI engine, thresholds, RQI = MISSING.

  ‚ĚĆ MISSING

  - Assessment batteries, gateways, crisis-hook ‚ÄĒ 0%.
  - Onboarding loop ‚ÄĒ syncOrgClaims, invite-accept, roster CSV, consent-capture
  screens, HR-Ops zone.
  - Infra/observability ‚ÄĒ Sentry, PostHog, Logtail, Resend, MSG91, Cloudflare,
  Redis cache = env-var-only or absent. ~30% deploy-ready.
  - Migrations NOT mirrored to md-latest / md-admin repos ‚ÄĒ they live only in
  moodscale-platform + local Docker.
  - Phases 2‚Äď7 ‚ÄĒ Health/Engagement/Impact tabs, QBR PDF ‚ÄĒ deferred.
  - Committed secrets to purge ‚ÄĒ .mcp.json token, .env.local files. Prod DB
  password OUMmsf1VsPayVQ2r still needs rotating.

  The real Phase-1 blockers (if the goal is a usable Phase-1)

  1. compute_metric_snapshot + remaining Kernel RPCs ‚ÄĒ without these, only
  participation works.
  2. Onboarding loop ‚ÄĒ no way for a real HR user to get an org, invite members,
  or capture consent through the UI.
  3. Migrations not mirrored to the two shared-DB repos ‚ÄĒ a deploy would diverge
  the schema.
  4. Assessment batteries ‚ÄĒ nothing for members to actually answer yet.

  Nothing was committed/pushed, and prod stays untouched (only your own password
  reset).

  Which area do you want next? My recommendation, in order: (1) mirror the
  migrations into the 3 repos so the schema can't diverge, then (2) build
  compute_metric_snapshot + the missing Kernel RPCs so metrics beyond
  participation compute, then (3) the onboarding/consent loop when you've signed
  up for Resend + Upstash.

‚ĚĮ Tell me if all this has been implemented?                                     
                                                                                
  The metric architecture is the back half of `doc 05` (¬ß4‚Äď5), which got        
  truncated when I read it. Let me pull it so the metrics list is authoritative 
  rather than pieced together from the QA hints.Here's the metric architecture  
  from `doc 05 ¬ß4` (cross-checked with the thresholds locked in `doc 10`/QA).   
  Metrics are organized by *class* ‚ÄĒ health outcomes (KHIs), trust/quality      
  (KTIs), and value/ROI ‚ÄĒ and everything rolls up through three tiers, with     
  nothing at the top hand-entered.                                              
                                                                                
  ## Headline health indicators (KHIs)                                          
                                                                                
  | Metric | Lead/lag | Inputs | Formula / shape | Bands |                      
  |---|---|---|---|---|                                                         
  | **OWI** ‚ÄĒ Organisational Wellbeing Index | Lagging (the headline) | WHO-5,  
  OLBI (inv), PSS (inv), PCI, low-severity prevalence | Weighted normalised     
  blend; weights versioned in `metric_definitions` | 0‚Äď100; Green ‚Č•70 / Amber   
  55‚Äď69 / Coral <55 (continuous gauge, coral never red) |                       
  | **BRI** ‚ÄĒ Burnout Risk Index | Lagging | OLBI exhaustion + disengagement |  
  Subscale composite, dept √ó quarter | 4 bands |                                
  | **Burnout Velocity** | **Leading** | BRI from prior snapshots | QoQ rate of 
  change: `BRI_t ‚ąí BRI_{t-1}` | őĒ amber ‚Č•8, red ‚Č•12 |                           
  | **VDI** ‚ÄĒ Vulnerability Distribution Index | Lagging | PHQ/GAD/severity     
  bands | % of cohort per band (Low/Mod/High/Critical); counts <k suppressed |  
  distribution shape |                                                          
  | **SLI/EI Quadrant** ‚ÄĒ Stress √ó Engagement | Diagnostic | PSS/stress √ó       
  UWES/engagement | Quadrant per dept: Thriving / Coasting / Straining /        
  Burning-out | quadrant |                                                      
  | **Attrition Risk Signal** | **Leading** | OLBI + UWES + RET-1               
  (intent-to-stay) | Modelled blend ‚Üí cohort flag | High/Med/Low ‚ÄĒ **L3 only,   
  k‚Č•5** |                                                                       
                                                                                
  ## Trust & data-quality indicators (KTIs)                                     
                                                                                
  The two governing ones are **TQ ‚ÄĒ Trust Quotient** (`participation √ó validity 
  √ó (1 ‚ąí divergence) √ó trust_item` ‚Üí 0‚Äď100) and **DCS ‚ÄĒ Data Confidence         
  Score** (the **geometric mean** of participation, validity and                
  representativeness, stamped on *every* snapshot; low DCS dims the dashboard   
  to "treat as directional," never hides it). Supporting these: Participation   
  Rate (‚Č•70% contract KPI), Decision Rate (complete + opt-out √∑ invited, ‚Č•95%), 
  Opt-Out Trend, Response Validity Rate (1 ‚ąí RQI-excluded, ‚Č•90%), Channel       
  Divergence Index, and Help-Seeking Conversion.                                
                                                                                
  ## Value / ROI metrics                                                        
                                                                                
  Three, all running on MoodScale-owned data (HRMS is a Phase-2 upsell, not a   
  dependency ‚ÄĒ QA L-11): **Presenteeism Cost** (WHO-HPQ hours √ó loaded cost),   
  **Programme ROI Multiple** (productivity + absence                            
  ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ (132 lines hidden) ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ 
  NACTIVE until the blend is modelled. visibility=L3_only must be enforced in   
  RLS/resolver, k>=5.                                                           
  ('ATTRITION_RISK','v0.9-pilot','Attrition Risk                                
  Signal','KHI','retention',1,'chro',                                           
   '{"inputs":["OLBI","UWES","RET1"],                                           
     "transform":"modelled_blend",                                              
     "output":"cohort_flag",                                                    
     "model_weights":"UNSET ‚ÄĒ pending modelling",                               
     "visibility":"L3_only"}'::jsonb,                                           
   '{"levels":["high","med","low"],"provisional":true}'::jsonb,                 
   null,5,'quarterly',false);                                                   
  ```                                                                           
                                                                                
  ## Notes that make the seed usable                                            
                                                                                
  The `formula` jsonb leans on a few **normalization helpers the worker has to  
  implement** before OWI/SLI can compute: `favourability_0_100` (the            
  `((mean‚ąí1)/4)√ó100` transform, with OLBI/PSS flipped via `direction:"-"`),     
  `native_0_100` (WHO-5's raw 0‚Äď25 √ó4), and `pct_healthy_0_100` for prevalence. 
  Those are the same `score_transform` flags `doc 05 ¬ß2.3` puts in              
  `scoring_algorithm` ‚ÄĒ reuse them, don't reinvent.                             
                                                                                
  Two **guardrail pairs** are seeded: `participation_validity` (Participation‚ÜĎ  
  must not drop Validity ‚ÄĒ both rows carry the key) and `owi_dcs` (never        
  publish OWI without its DCS confidence stamp). `engagement_stepdown` is       
  referenced on BRI but its partner (a Healthy Step-Down metric) isn't in       
  Phase-1 scope ‚ÄĒ leave it dangling or drop the key until that metric exists.   
                                                                                
  A couple of **class labels I inferred** and you should confirm against `doc   
  10`'s taxonomy (KHI/KTI/KCI/KPI/KRI): I used `KCI` for DCS (confidence) and   
  `KTI` for participation, though participation is also described as the        
  contract *KPI* ‚ÄĒ pick one and be consistent. And the one **KRI** worth        
  registering separately is the suppression-violation tripwire                  
  ("suppression-rule violations = zero, ever" ‚ÄĒ `doc 05 ¬ß8`); that's an         
  operational alarm, not a `snapshot_cells` metric, so it belongs in your       
  monitoring/audit layer rather than this seed.                                 
                                                                                
  Net: of these, `PARTICIPATION_PCT` is the only one with both a definition     
  *and* a working compute path today; `RESPONSE_VALIDITY_RATE`,                 
  `TRUST_QUOTIENT`, `DCS`, and `VDI` become live the moment their input         
  instruments are seeded and a campaign freezes; everything else waits on a     
  sign-off, a norm, a prior snapshot, or a model.                               
                                                                                
  Want me to write the matching **`computeXCells` worker functions** for the    
  activatable ones (validity, TQ, DCS, VDI) in the same shape as the existing   
  `computeParticipationCells` ‚ÄĒ pure, k‚Č•5-suppressed, unit-tested ‚ÄĒ so the      
  registry rows have compute to back them? I can also hand you this seed as a   
  `.sql` file if you'd prefer it saved rather than inline.

  The architecture rules

  - k‚Č•5 + complementary suppression ‚ÄĒ ‚úÖ done (SQL fixpoint, proven).
  - Compute only at freeze ‚ÄĒ ‚úÖ done (compute_metric_snapshot runs at campaign
  close).
  - Weights in definition, not code ‚ÄĒ ‚úÖ structurally (OWI weights live in
  formula jsonb)‚Ä¶ but ‚ö†ÔłŹ they're placeholders and the row is active.
  - One versioned row per metric ‚ÄĒ ūüü° the registry exists, but the table is 
  missing columns your seed assumes: there is no class, no guardrail_pair_key, 
  no forum, no effective_from, no visibility, and the key column is key, not
  metric_key.
  - Guardrail pairs ‚ÄĒ ‚ĚĆ not modelled (no column to hold the pair key).
  - Tier 3‚Üí2‚Üí1 rollup lineage ‚ÄĒ ūüü° tiers are labelled and org/dept/level grains
  compute, but there's no enforced rollup traceability.
  - KRI suppression tripwire ‚ÄĒ ‚ĚĆ not built (it's a monitoring-layer alarm).

  Two things that directly affect your pasted seed

  1. It won't apply as-is. It inserts into metric_key, class, 
  guardrail_pair_key, forum, effective_from ‚ÄĒ none of which are columns. You'd
  need either a migration to add those columns, or to remap the seed onto the
  real shape (key, family, tier, formula, bands, owner_role, is_active).
  2. My OWI is active with unratified weights ‚ÄĒ your seed correctly sets
  is_active=false for OWI/BRI/velocity/quadrant/attrition. Mine doesn't. That's
  a real discrepancy I should fix.

  Net: of your ~16 metrics, VDI and Participation are truly done end-to-end;
  OWI, OBI/BRI, ROI-multiple are computed but provisional (placeholder weights /
  synthetic inputs / wrong key); DCS and Validity are registry-only; TQ, 
  Velocity, SLI/EI, Attrition-as-a-signal, Recovery Yield, Decision Rate, 
  Opt-Out, Divergence, Help-Seeking are not built. And the registry schema
  itself needs the class/guardrail_pair_key/forum/visibility/effective_from
  columns before your seed is usable.

  Want me to (a) add those registry columns + reconcile the seed, (b) flip
  OWI/BRI/etc. to is_active=false to match your sign-off rule, and (c) build the
  computeValidity/TQ/DCS worker paths so the KTI quality suite stops being
  registry-only?

  - DCS ‚ÄĒ geomean(participation, validity, representativeness‚Čąparticipation) ‚Üí
  stamped on the snapshot header (83.6) + an org cell.

  The "‚Č•2 independent flags ‚áí excluded" rule is enforced ‚ÄĒ a single
  co-occurrence stays valid. Each session's trail is stored in a new
  campaign_member_scores.rqi_flags jsonb for auditability. The worker runs it
  after projection, before metrics, so excluded sessions drop out of
  aggregation.

  Proven on Acme Q2

  - 17 members ‚Üí 5 excluded (ENG-8 had 3 flags; ENG-1/2 & SAL-1/3 had¬†2). ENG-4
  and EXE-2 (1 flag each) stay valid.
  - Validity stopped being a ceiling: org 70.6% (was 100%), Engineering 62.5%,
  l2 0%.
  - OWI now means the valid cohort: org n dropped 17 ‚Üí 12.
  - DCS propagated it: 83.6 ‚Üí 74.5 through the geomean.

  The asymmetry holds (the load-bearing bit)

  compute_rqi writes only campaign_member_scores.valid / .rqi_flags ‚ÄĒ an
  aggregation exclusion. It never touches crisis_event. The PHQ-9 item-9 hook
  fires on user_assessments independently and is never retracted by an RQI flag.
  Verified: 5 RQI-excluded members, 0 crisis rows touched.

  Honest remaining edges

  - The level-module pairs (WLI/WD/SP/EX, OLBI-exhaustion√óUWES-Vigor, ISI√ópulse)
  are specced but inactive until those instruments project into member scores ‚ÄĒ
  so the engine currently runs 5 of the doc's ~7 pair families.
  - The thresholds (who5‚Č•70, phq9/gad7‚Č•15, pss‚Č•68/<35, olbi‚Č•70) are reasonable
  defaults, not yet clinically ratified.

  Want me next to (1) surface Validity/TQ/DCS on a "Data Confidence" dashboard
  strip (add them to the GraphQL MetricKey enum + a panel), or (2) project the
  level-module instruments so the remaining RQI pairs activate?

‚Źļ All three threads are done, verified, and documented. Local only, no prod, no
  commits.

  A ‚ÄĒ Synthetic inputs hardened into the real assessment flow

  The pipeline no longer seeds campaign_member_scores directly. The real path
  now runs:

  local auth.users ‚Üí org_members.user_id + identity map ‚Üí assessment_results 
  (stamped campaign_id, with section_scores) ‚Üí project_campaign_member_scores + 
  project_campaign_pulse ‚Üí RQI ‚Üí metrics ‚Üí quality

  Score values are still synthetic (no live respondents), but the flow is real ‚ÄĒ
  including the engine's own validate_assessment_results /
  validate_assessment_severity triggers firing on insert. Proven: the worker
  close drives everything from projected data:
  - rqi: "excluded 9" (the exact crafted set, every member with its pair),
  - OWI 55.7, validity 47.1%, TQ 28.1, VDI moderate 100%, DCS 69.9.

  (One real bug caught and cleared along the way: an early "VDI critical"
  reading was a stale-read artifact ‚ÄĒ a clean deterministic run confirms
  moderate, which is correct for the valid baseline cohort.)

  B ‚ÄĒ Remaining dashboard tab

  Engagement is now wired to real participation (the one fully-computed metric):
  completion by department and level against the 70% contract floor,
  depts-at-target, and a suppressed-cohort count. Live: org 76.5% (n=17),
  Engineering 87.5% visible, Sales/Exec + L2/L3 suppressed (k‚Č•5). The
  therapy-utilisation funnel is honestly deferred (needs booking data) rather
  than faked. All four tabs (Overview, Health & Risk, Engagement, Impact) + the
  Data Confidence strip now render real data.

  - New IMPLEMENTATION-STATUS.md ‚ÄĒ a current-state snapshot (metrics/registry
  with active-vs-inactive, RQI 7/7, crisis-hook, privacy, dashboard, onboarding,
  and an honest "still synthetic/pending" section).
  - 00-B2B-INDEX.md now points to it up top.
  - QA.md ¬ß35 logs this work (BL-34/35/36).

  Honest caveats (carried in the docs)

  - Result rows are labelled assessment_type='custom' (PHQ-9/GAD-7 included)
  because per-type interpretation configs (severity bands) aren't seeded ‚ÄĒ
  template_id preserves instrument identity, which the projection keys on.
  Seeding real severity configs is a later refinement.
  - ROI still runs on a synthetic HPQ baseline; thresholds (OWI weights, RQI
  cutoffs) remain defaults pending clinical ratification; OWI stays hidden
  (inactive) until weights are signed off.

  The measurement/quality engine is now genuinely end-to-end on the real flow.
  Good place to pause ‚ÄĒ the next natural steps would be seeding real PHQ-9/GAD-7
  interpretation configs (so results carry proper severity bands), or moving to
  the parked infra (Resend invite emails, Redis cache).

  templates are now first-class interpretable, not orphaned.
  - Real flow now emits PHQ-9/GAD-7 results with assessment_type='phq9'/'gad7' +
  the real severity_key, and the engine's own validate_assessment_severity() 
  trigger validates them on insert (the real clinical guardrail, not a bypass).

  Proven

  - PHQ-9 results: 12 mild + 5 moderately_severe (the 5 crafted high-PHQ members
  correctly band as moderately_severe).
  - GAD-7 results: 16 mild + 1 severe (ENG-1 with gad7=17 ‚Üí severe).
  - Worker close unchanged: rqi: "excluded 9", all metrics compute ‚ÄĒ severity
  bands don't perturb the aggregation, they ride alongside it.

  The earlier custom/computed placeholder is gone; the demo's clinical results
  now carry validated bands. 24 migrations mirrored across all three repos; docs
  updated (IMPLEMENTATION-STATUS clinical section + QA.md ¬ß36).

  That closes the loop on the real assessment flow ‚ÄĒ the only remaining
  synthetic element is the response values themselves (no live humans), which is
  inherent to a demo. Natural next steps if you want them: seed real
  interpretation configs for the remaining instruments (OLBI/PSS/ISI bands), or

‚Źļ The member take-flow is built, proven end-to-end, and mirrored. Local only, no
  prod, no commits.

  What was built

  Migration 27 ‚ÄĒ submit_campaign_battery(campaign, user_id, responses) ‚ÄĒ the
  authoritative scorer in SQL:
  - Gateway-aware: only the items actually administered are summed, so PHQ-2‚Üí9 /
  GAD-2‚Üí7 branching is real (closed gate ‚Üí 2-item score; open gate ‚Üí full
  instrument).
  - Reads question metadata: applies reverse-scoring and computes section means
  from assessment_questions (no hardcoding).
  - Writes one assessment_results per instrument (stamped campaign_id, with
  section_scores) + a user_assessments session per instrument (which fires the 
  crisis trigger on PHQ-9 item-9), and completes the assignment.

  md-latest take-flow (typecheck clean):
  - GET /api/org/campaign/battery ‚ÄĒ serves the member's pending battery +
  gateway rules
  - POST /api/org/campaign/submit ‚ÄĒ self-scoped (p_user_id = auth.uid()) ‚Üí the
  RPC
  - (protected)/(org)/campaign/take ‚ÄĒ member page that unfolds PHQ-9/GAD-7 only
  when the gate opens

  Proven end-to-end (then rolled back, demo state intact)

  A full submission:
  - scored 13 instruments ‚ÄĒ who5 ‚Üí good_wellbeing (raw¬†20), phq9 ‚Üí moderate via 
  open gateway (raw¬†13), gad7 ‚Üí minimal via closed gateway (raw¬†2), isi ‚Üí none,
  trust1 ‚Üí thriving
  - reverse-scoring verified: OLBI disengagement mean = 3 from raw-2 answers;
  sections exhaustion 2.0 / disengagement 3.0
  - projected into pseudonym-space scores with subscores
  - crisis fired on the submitted item-9 (screening_flag)
  - assignment marked completed

  What this closes

  battery now drives assessment_results ‚Üí projection ‚Üí RQI ‚Üí metrics through the
  real scorer ‚ÄĒ gateway branching, reverse-scoring, sectioning, and the
  crisis-hook all real ‚ÄĒ instead of directly seeded scores. The only thing still
  synthetic is the answer values themselves (no live humans), which is inherent

‚Źļ Campaign scheduling + reminders are built, proven end-to-end, and mirrored.
  Local only, no prod, no commits.

  What was built

  Migration 28 ‚ÄĒ the campaign lifecycle state machine + reminder engine
  (deterministic via a p_now param, so it's testable; actual sends stay parked,
  events logged):
  - open_campaign ‚ÄĒ scheduled‚Üíopen, creates campaign_assignments for the active
  audience.
  - send_due_reminders ‚ÄĒ nudges non-responders per
  reminder_schedule.offsets_days, increments reminder_count/last_reminded_at,
  moves assigned‚Üínotified (send PARKED ‚Üí logged).
  - close_campaign ‚ÄĒ open‚Üíclosed, expires anyone who didn't finish.
  - tick_campaigns(now) ‚ÄĒ the scheduler: open due ‚Üí remind due ‚Üí close due.
  - New campaign_events audit table (service-role-only ‚ÄĒ per-member reminder
  rows are never employer-readable, preserving the Iron Rule; HR sees the
  aggregate roster instead).

  Worker integration ‚ÄĒ runScheduler (scheduler.ts + tick-local.ts) ticks the
  state machine, then auto-aggregates any freshly-closed campaign that lacks a
  published snapshot.

  Proven end-to-end

  Lifecycle (ticked across time): opens at window-start (17 assignments) ‚Üí
  reminder #1 to all 17 ‚Üí 5 complete ‚Üí reminder #2 to the remaining 12
  (completers drop out) ‚Üí closes after window, expires the 12 non-responders.
  Audit trail: opened(1) / closed(1) / reminder(41, incl. a final pre-close
  nudge).

  Auto-aggregation on close: runScheduler @ 2026-07-15 ‚Üí closed: 1, then
  aggregated: [{period: 2026-Q3, status: computed}] ‚Üí Q3 snapshot published,
  participation 62.5% (5 of 8). Then cleaned up.

  Honest notes

  - Reminder sends are PARKED ‚ÄĒ the engine computes who's due and logs a
  campaign_events row per nudge; it doesn't email/SMS yet (needs Resend/MSG91).
  - The deployed worker runs runScheduler on a repeatable BullMQ job (needs
  Redis ‚ÄĒ parked); locally it's tick-local.ts.
  - reminder_schedule shape is {"offsets_days":[3,7,10]} (days after
  window-start); easy to make per-org.

  28 migrations mirrored across all three repos; QA.md ¬ß40 +
  IMPLEMENTATION-STATUS.md updated.

  This closes the campaign-lifecycle gap: campaigns now open, nudge, and close 
  on a schedule, and aggregate themselves on close ‚ÄĒ the last piece of the
  Phase-1 measurement loop that wasn't automated. The remaining items are the
  parked infra (Resend/Redis/observability), the cheap inactive metrics
  (Decision Rate, Presenteeism Cost), benchmarking, and governance sign-offs.
  Want me to knock out the cheap inactive metrics next, or wire Resend so
  reminders + invites actually send?

‚Źļ The member "Me" wellbeing dashboard is built ‚ÄĒ Phase 2's last gap closed.
  Local only, md-latest code (no migration), no prod, no commits.

  Why this was the easiest high-value pick

  - Real data already exists ‚ÄĒ the take-flow now produces banded results, so
  there was nothing to seed.
  - Zero parked infra ‚ÄĒ no Resend/Redis/Cloudflare/observability needed (those
  gate the other options).
  - Self-contained ‚ÄĒ one API route + one page in md-latest.
  - Completes a phase ‚ÄĒ it's the one member-facing surface that was missing.

  What was built

  - GET /api/org/me/results ‚ÄĒ strictly self-scoped (user_id = auth.uid()):
  returns the member's own latest banded results per instrument, org name,
  pending-campaign flag, and their consent summary. This is the only place
  individual scores appear ‚ÄĒ to the person themselves; the employer never sees
  it.
  - (protected)/(org)/me page ‚ÄĒ the member's wellbeing snapshot:
    - Friendly instrument names (Overall wellbeing, Mood, Stress, Sleep,
  Burnout, Work‚Äďlife balance, ‚Ä¶) with their band + a progress bar.
    - Calm member-facing colours ‚ÄĒ never red (doc 10 ¬ß2.1): green / amber /
  coral (a calm rose for "could use support"), enforcing the employee-facing
  rule.
    - A "Take your check-in" CTA when a campaign is pending (‚Üí the take-flow).
    - A supportive "It can help to talk to someone" panel when any band is
  elevated ‚Üí routes to sessions, with the reassurance that booking is private.
    - A consent-management link (‚Üí the consent-capture screen).
    - The privacy reassurance up top: "Only you can see this. Your employer only
  ever sees anonymous group results."

  Proven

  - tsc --noEmit clean.
  - A member (ENG-7) has 14 banded results ready to render ‚ÄĒ Overall wellbeing ‚Üí
  Moderate, Stress ‚Üí Moderate, Burnout ‚Üí Moderate, Trust ‚Üí Thriving, etc. ‚ÄĒ
  exactly what the endpoint serves.

  (I didn't run a live browser smoke test because the member surface uses
  cookie-session auth rather than the Bearer tokens I can mint headlessly; the
  data-layer query is verified and the page typechecks.)

  Docs updated: IMPLEMENTATION-STATUS (Phase 2 now complete) + QA.md ¬ß41.

  Where that leaves the roadmap

  Phase 2 is now done. The remaining gaps are the ones that genuinely need
  parked infra or are larger surfaces: Phase 0
  (secrets/Resend/Redis/observability/Cloudflare), Phase 4 reporting/UI (QBR
  PDF, HR Campaign Control UI, heatmaps/trends/benchmark widgets, DO/Redis), and
  Phases 5‚Äď7.

  Of what's left without parked infra, the next-easiest are the QBR/Org-Health 
  PDF (self-contained, just needs a PDF lib) or the heatmap widget (reuses
  existing dept metric cells). Want me to take one of those?

‚Źļ Both done. Local only, no prod, no commits.

  Fix: the "No valid session" error

  That was the same JWT issue from earlier surfacing in your browser. The
  running API had been verifying tokens against a leaked test-secret ‚ÄĒ a build
  step had export SUPABASE_JWT_SECRET=‚Ä¶, and Node's --env-file doesn't override 
  an already-exported env var, so the API ignored .env's real secret. Since real
  GoTrue login tokens are signed with the real local secret, the API rejected
  them ‚Üí "No valid session."

  I confirmed GoTrue's secret (super-secret‚Ä¶), issuer, and audience, restarted
  the API cleanly (env -u SUPABASE_JWT_SECRET ‚Ä¶) so it now uses the matching
  secret, and verified the exact failing overview query returns data again.

  ‚Üí Hard-refresh the dashboard (‚Ćė‚áßR) and the error is gone. One thing you'll
  notice: OWI shows blank/"pending" on Overview ‚ÄĒ that's expected, because you
  had me set OWI inactive pending sign-off. To show it, run: update 
  public.metric_definitions set is_active=true where key='OWI'; (re-run a worker
  close after).

  HR Campaign Control UI

  Built in md-admin's HR-Ops zone (/admin/org-admin/[orgId]/campaigns), wiring
  the migration-28 scheduler to a screen:

  - Create ‚ÄĒ name, period, window dates, reminder offsets; defaults to the
  Common-Core battery, status scheduled.

  org_admin/hr_ops).

  What was built (Phase 5)

  Migration 29 ‚ÄĒ get_team_home(user_id, period) ‚ÄĒ the manager-scoped Kernel RPC
  with the strict L2 privacy model:
  - Own team only ‚ÄĒ the team is derived in-DB from the caller, so a manager
  can't request another team.
  - k‚Č•5 ‚ÄĒ a sub-5 team returns suppressed, no aggregate.
  - Directions, not values ‚ÄĒ returns the wellbeing band (green/amber/coral),
  never the raw OWI number, plus participation%, validity%, and a coaching
  Finding + Play.
  - Seeded org_teams (Engineering/Sales/Executive) and assigned members.

  AAL2, allowlisted, schema regenerated, 7/7 tests (privacy walk confirms no
  individual fields).

  calm-coloured direction, participation/size, and the Finding/Play in a

  What was built (Phase 6)

  Detection was already done (the PHQ-9 item-9 trigger ‚Üí crisis_event). This
  adds the human response side:

  Migration 30 ‚ÄĒ crisis ops (all service-role guarded ‚ÄĒ the single sanctioned 
  re-identification path):
  - crisis_queue() ‚ÄĒ open events ordered imminent ‚Üí passive ‚Üí screening, with
  identity resolved for outreach + age/SLA.
  - crisis_log_attempt() ‚ÄĒ appends to the medico-legal attempt trail (channel ¬∑
  time ¬∑ outcome).
  - crisis_set_disposition() ‚ÄĒ the R1/R2/R3 ladder (+ monitoring).
  - crisis_resolve() ‚ÄĒ closes the case.

  md-admin duty-clinician UI (/admin/crisis, super_admin only):
  - Queue with SLA badges (imminent = same-day / alert >4h; passive 24‚Äď48h /
  alert >48h).
  - Per-row R1/R2/R3 disposition select, "Log call" (attempt + outcome),
  Resolve, and an expandable attempt history.
  - API routes (GET queue + PATCH [id]) self-authorize to super_admin and call
  the service-role RPCs.

  Proven

  - Queue returns 3 open cases ordered by severity with member names + age;
  logging an attempt + setting R2 worked; resolve removed it from the queue 
  (3‚Üí2).
  - Privacy held: a CHRO (employer) calling crisis_queue() gets "forbidden" ‚ÄĒ
  the queue is Tier-1 internal, never employer-facing. crisis_event still has no
  employer RLS policy.
  - Typecheck clean.

  The load-bearing principle, intact

  The crisis queue is the only place re-identification happens ‚ÄĒ through
  service-role Kernel functions, for clinical outreach only, behind a
  super_admin gate. 100% human, employers never see it. RQI/aggregation never
  touch this path (the asymmetry from earlier still holds).

  Why it was empty

  derives the team from auth.uid() in-DB, so a caller can only ever see their 
  own team, at k‚Č•5 ‚ÄĒ the privacy boundary holds regardless of role. (In

  is fine.)

  isn't consented/scored, so it doesn't distort the aggregate; it just gives you
  a team to view.

‚Źļ The "How it works" guide is built, wired into the nav, and typecheck-clean.
  Local only, no migration, no prod, no commits.

  What I built ‚ÄĒ the /guide "How it works" tab

  A comprehensive, plain-English in-product explainer (new nav item "How it 
  works"), grounded in exactly what the platform actually does. Nine sections:

  1. The one rule ‚ÄĒ the Iron Rule, with a side-by-side "‚úÖ you CAN see / ūüöę you
  can NEVER see," and the point that it's enforced in the database, not just
  promised.
  2. When does data appear? ‚ÄĒ the campaign lifecycle (scheduled ‚Üí opens ‚Üí people
  respond ‚Üí closes & freezes ‚Üí you see it) plus a "what shows when" table: any
  metric needs a frozen snapshot; a dept/team/level cell needs 5+ respondents;
  My Teams needs the manager's team at 5+; trends need 2 quarters; ROI needs a
  baseline; benchmarks need 8+ orgs; OWI needs sign-off.
  3. Every metric, and how it's calculated ‚ÄĒ Participation, OWI, VDI, Validity,
  Trust Quotient, DCS, ROI, BRI ‚ÄĒ each with its formula, bands, and a live / 
  pending badge (so the blank OWI is explained, not mysterious).
  4. How a single number is built ‚ÄĒ the 7-step pipeline, calling out exactly
  where identity is dropped (the structural firewall).
  5. Why some numbers say "treat as directional" ‚ÄĒ participation/validity
  (RQI)/representativeness, and that safety is never affected by quality flags.
  6. What each screen shows ‚ÄĒ Overview, Health & Risk, Engagement, Impact,
  Participation, My Teams, the Data Confidence strip, the Org Health Report.
  7. Privacy & safety in practice ‚ÄĒ per-purpose consent, private crisis
  handling, erasure, the single re-identification path.
  8. The advantages ‚ÄĒ honest answers ‚Üí real signal, privacy by construction,
  confidence on every number, safety without surveillance, managers
  coach-not-police, measurable ROI.
  9. FAQ ‚ÄĒ the exact questions you've hit ("Why is OWI blank?", "Why 'below
  threshold'?", "Why did Validity drop?", "When will my team show up?").

  Also: I fixed "My Teams shows nothing" from the previous turn

  You're logged in as hr@acme.test (hr_ops, no team). I broadened teamHome to
  employer roles (still own-team-only + k‚Č•5 ‚ÄĒ the team is derived from
  auth.uid(), so no leak) and attached the HR accounts to the Engineering Team.
  Verified live: {status: ok, team: "Engineering Team", n: 8, participation 
  87.5%, wellbeing amber, ‚Ä¶}.

  Hard-refresh the dashboard ‚ÄĒ you'll see a new "How it works" tab in the top
  nav, and My Teams now populated.

‚ĚĮ Please use these UI guidelines: # UI Fixes Guide                              
                                                                                
  ## 1. Button Glow Effect Fix                                                  
                                                                                
  ### The Problem                                                               
  By default, some UI component libraries (like shadcn/ui) add a box-shadow to  
  buttons which creates a "glow" effect. This is more visible in dark mode      
  where it appears as a light halo around buttons.                              
                                                                                
  ### The Fix                                                                   
  Add these Tailwind classes to your button:                                    
  ```                                                                           
  shadow-none hover:shadow-none transition-all duration-200 hover:scale-105     
  ```                                                                           
                                                                                
  ### What Each Class Does                                                      
  | Class | Purpose |                                                           
  |-------|---------|                                                           
  | `shadow-none` | Removes the default shadow/glow |                           
  | `hover:shadow-none` | Removes shadow/glow on hover |                        
  | `transition-all duration-200` | Smooth animation (200ms) |                  
  | `hover:scale-105` | Subtle 5% scale-up effect on hover |                    
                                                                                
  ### Example                                                                   
  ```tsx                                                                        
  // Before                                                                     
  <Button className="bg-[#1E3A5F] hover:bg-[#162d4a] text-white">               
    Click Me                                                                    
  </Button>                                                                     
                                                                                
  // After                                                                      
  <Button className="bg-[#1E3A5F] hover:bg-[#162d4a] text-white shadow-none     
  hover:shadow-none transition-all duration-200 hover:scale-105">               
    Click Me                                                                    
  </Button>                                                                     
                                                                                
  // For Outline Buttons                                                        
  <Button variant="outline" className="shadow-none hover:shadow-none            
  transition-all duration-200 hover:scale-105">                                 
    Cancel                                                                      
  </Button>                                                                     
  ```                                                                           
                                                                                
  ---                                                                           
                                                                                
  ## 2. Native Dropdown/Select Fix                                              
                                                                                
  ### The Problem                                                               
  Native HTML `<select>` elements use the operating system's default dropdown   
  UI (e.g., macOS native dropdown). This looks inconsistent with the app's      
  custom styling, especially in dark mode.                                      
                                                                                
  ### The Fix                                                                   
  Replace native `<select>` with shadcn/ui `DropdownMenu` component.            
                                                                                
  ### Before (Native Select - Bad)                                              
  ```tsx                                                                        
  <select                                                                       
    value={filter}                                                              
    onChange={(e) => setFilter(e.target.value)}                                 
    className="border rounded-lg px-3 py-2 bg-white dark:bg-slate-800"          
  >                                                                             
    <option value="all">All Items</option>                                      
    <option value="active">Active</option>                                      
  </select>                                                                     
  ```                                                                           
                                                                                
  ### After (Custom DropdownMenu - Good)                                        
  ```tsx                                                                        
  import { DropdownMenu, DropdownMenuContent, DropdownMenuItem,                 
  DropdownMenuTrigger } from '@/components/ui/dropdown-menu'                    
  import { ChevronDown } from 'lucide-react'                                    
                                                                                
  <DropdownMenu>                                                                
    <DropdownMenuTrigger asChild>                                               
      <Button                                                                   
        variant="outline"                                                       
        className="justify-between min-w-[140px] bg-white dark:bg-slate-800     
  border-slate-200 dark:border-slate-600 text-slate-800 dark:text-white         
  hover:bg-slate-50 dark:hover:bg-slate-700 shadow-none hover:shadow-none       
  transition-all duration-200 hover:scale-105"                                  
      >                                                                         
        {filter === 'all' ? 'All Items' : 'Active'}                             
        <ChevronDown className="h-4 w-4 opacity-50" />                          
      </Button>                                                                 
    </DropdownMenuTrigger>                                                      
    <DropdownMenuConten                                                         
  ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ (189 lines hidden) ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ 
  body`) | `bg-white dark:bg-slate-900 divide-y divide-slate-200                
  dark:divide-slate-700` |                                                      
  | Table Row (`tr`) | `hover:bg-slate-50 dark:hover:bg-slate-800/50` |         
  | Primary Text | `text-sm font-medium text-slate-900 dark:text-white` |       
  | Secondary Text | `text-sm text-slate-500 dark:text-slate-400` |             
                                                                                
  ### Type Badge in Table                                                       
  ```tsx                                                                        
  <span className="inline-flex items-center px-2.5 py-0.5 rounded-md text-xs    
  font-medium bg-slate-100 text-slate-700 dark:bg-slate-700                     
  dark:text-slate-300">                                                         
    Badge Text                                                                  
  </span>                                                                       
  ```                                                                           
                                                                                
  ### Action Buttons in Table                                                   
  ```tsx                                                                        
  <div className="flex items-center justify-end gap-1">                         
    <Button variant="outline" size="sm" className="shadow-none                  
  hover:shadow-none transition-all duration-200 hover:scale-105">               
      <Download className="w-4 h-4" />                                          
    </Button>                                                                   
  </div>                                                                        
  ```                                                                           
                                                                                
  ### Pages Using This Pattern

  - `/assessment-results` - Assessment results table                            
                                                                                
  ---                                                                           
                                                                                
  ## 7. General Guidelines                                                      
                                                                                
  ### No Comments in Code                                                       
  When making changes or adding code, do not add any comments. Keep the code    
  clean and self-explanatory without inline comments or documentation blocks.   
                                                                                
  ### No Emojis                                                                 
  Do not use emojis anywhere in the UI. Keep the interface clean and            
  professional without any emoji characters.                                    
                                                                                
  ---                                                                           
                                                                                
  ## 8. Invoice & Payment Terminology                                           
                                                                                
  Use consistent terminology across all invoices, payment descriptions, and     
  related UI.                                                                   
                                                                                
  ### Standard Terms                                                            
                                                                                
  | Old Term | New Term |                                                       
  |----------|----------|                                                       
  | Mental Health Assessment | **Psychological Assessment** |                   
  | Credit Add-on Pack | **Credit Top-up Pack** |                               
  | Mental Health Service | **Psychological Services** |                        
  | Therapy Session Booking | **Therapy Session** |                             
                                                                                
  ### Keep As-Is                                                                
  - Transformative Care Package                                                 
  - Premium Journey Package                                                     
  - Essential Care Package                                                      
  - Assessment Pack (actual addon name from database)                           
                                                                                
  ### Usage in Code                                                             
  ```tsx

  itemDescription: `${assessmentName} - Psychological Assessment`               
                                                                                
  invoiceType: 'credit_addon'                                                   
  itemDescription: `${addon.display_name} - Credit Top-up Pack`                 
                                                                                
  invoiceType: 'session'                                                        
  itemDescription: 'Therapy Session'                                            
  ```

  - `src/app/api/payments/verify-assessment-purchase/route.ts`                  
  - `src/app/api/payments/protected-assessment-purchase/route.ts`               
  - `src/app/api/payments/razorpay-webhook/route.ts`                            
  - `src/app/api/payments/credit-addon/route.ts`                                
  - `src/services/invoice/templates/creditAddonInvoiceTemplate.ts`

  http://localhost:3000/dashboard all these UI guidelines:                      
                                                                                
  # UI Fixes Guide                                                              
                                                                                
  ## 1. Button Glow Effect Fix                                                  
                                                                                
  ### The Problem                                                               
  By default, some UI component libraries (like shadcn/ui) add a box-shadow to  
  buttons which creates a "glow" effect. This is more visible in dark mode      
  where it appears as a light halo around buttons.                              
                                                                                
  ### The Fix                                                                   
  Add these Tailwind classes to your button:                                    
  ```                                                                           
  shadow-none hover:shadow-none transition-all duration-200 hover:scale-105     
  ```                                                                           
                                                                                
  ### What Each Class Does                                                      
  | Class | Purpose |                                                           
  |-------|---------|                                                           
  | `shadow-none` | Removes the default shadow/glow |                           
  | `hover:shadow-none` | Removes shadow/glow on hover |                        
  | `transition-all duration-200` | Smooth animation (200ms) |                  
  | `hover:scale-105` | Subtle 5% scale-up effect on hover |                    
                                                                                
  ### Example                                                                   
  ```tsx                                                                        
  // Before                                                                     
  <Button className="bg-[#1E3A5F] hover:bg-[#162d4a] text-white">               
    Click Me                                                                    
  </Button>                                                                     
                                                                                
  // After                                                                      
  <Button className="bg-[#1E3A5F] hover:bg-[#162d4a] text-white shadow-none     
  hover:shadow-none transition-all duration-200 hover:scale-105">               
    Click Me                                                                    
  </Button>                                                                     
                                                                                
  // For Outline Buttons                                                        
  <Button variant="outline" className="shadow-none hover:shadow-none            
  transition-all duration-200 hover:scale-105">                                 
    Cancel                                                                      
  </Button>                                                                     
  ```                                                                           
                                                                                
  ---                                                                           
                                                                                
  ## 2. Native Dropdown/Select Fix                                              
                                                                                
  ### The Problem                                                               
  Native HTML `<select>` elements use the operating system's default dropdown   
  UI (e.g., macOS native dropdown). This looks inconsistent with the app's      
  custom styling, especially in dark mode.                                      
                                                                                
  ### The Fix                                                                   
  Replace native `<select>` with shadcn/ui `DropdownMenu` component.            
                                                                                
  ### Before (Native Select - Bad)                                              
  ```tsx                                                                        
  <select                                                                       
    value={filter}                                                              
    onChange={(e) => setFilter(e.target.value)}                                 
    className="border rounded-lg px-3 py-2 bg-white dark:bg-slate-800"          
  >                                                                             
    <option value="all">All Items</option>                                      
    <option value="active">Active</option>                                      
  </select>                                                                     
  ```                                                                           
                                                                                
  ### After (Custom DropdownMenu - Good)                                        
  ```tsx                                                                        
  import { DropdownMenu, DropdownMenuContent, DropdownMenuItem,                 
  DropdownMenuTrigger } from '@/components/ui/dropdown-menu'                    
  import { ChevronDown } from 'lucide-react'                                    
                                                                                
  <DropdownMenu>                                                                
    <DropdownMenuTrigger asChild>                                               
      <Button                                                                   
        variant="outline"                                                       
        className="justify-between min-w-[140px] bg-white dark:bg-slate-800     
  border-slate-200 dark:border-slate-600 text-slate-800 dark:text-white         
  hover:bg-slate-50 dark:hover:bg-slate-700 shadow-none hover:shadow-none       
  transition-all duration-200 hover:scale-105"                                  
      >                                                                         
        {filter === 'all' ? 'All Items' : 'Active'}                             
        <ChevronDown className="h-4                                             
  ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ (192 lines hidden) ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ 
  body`) | `bg-white dark:bg-slate-900 divide-y divide-slate-200                
  dark:divide-slate-700` |                                                      
  | Table Row (`tr`) | `hover:bg-slate-50 dark:hover:bg-slate-800/50` |         
  | Primary Text | `text-sm font-medium text-slate-900 dark:text-white` |       
  | Secondary Text | `text-sm text-slate-500 dark:text-slate-400` |             
                                                                                
  ### Type Badge in Table                                                       
  ```tsx                                                                        
  <span className="inline-flex items-center px-2.5 py-0.5 rounded-md text-xs    
  font-medium bg-slate-100 text-slate-700 dark:bg-slate-700                     
  dark:text-slate-300">                                                         
    Badge Text                                                                  
  </span>                                                                       
  ```                                                                           
                                                                                
  ### Action Buttons in Table                                                   
  ```tsx                                                                        
  <div className="flex items-center justify-end gap-1">                         
    <Button variant="outline" size="sm" className="shadow-none                  
  hover:shadow-none transition-all duration-200 hover:scale-105">               
      <Download className="w-4 h-4" />                                          
    </Button>                                                                   
  </div>                                                                        
  ```                                                                           
                                                                                
  ### Pages Using This Pattern                                                  
  - `/dashboard/invoices` - Invoice list table                                  
  - `/assessment-results` - Assessment results table                            
                                                                                
  ---                                                                           
                                                                                
  ## 7. General Guidelines                                                      
                                                                                
  ### No Comments in Code                                                       
  When making changes or adding code, do not add any comments. Keep the code    
  clean and self-explanatory without inline comments or documentation blocks.   
                                                                                
  ### No Emojis                                                                 
  Do not use emojis anywhere in the UI. Keep the interface clean and            
  professional without any emoji characters.                                    
                                                                                
  ---                                                                           
                                                                                
  ## 8. Invoice & Payment Terminology                                           
                                                                                
  Use consistent terminology across all invoices, payment descriptions, and     
  related UI.                                                                   
                                                                                
  ### Standard Terms                                                            
                                                                                
  | Old Term | New Term |                                                       
  |----------|----------|

  | Credit Add-on Pack | **Credit Top-up Pack** |                               
  | Mental Health Service | **Psychological Services** |                        
  | Therapy Session Booking | **Therapy Session** |                             
                                                                                
  ### Keep As-Is                                                                
  - Transformative Care Package                                                 
  - Premium Journey Package                                                     
  - Essential Care Package                                                      
  - Assessment Pack (actual addon name from database)                           
                                                                                
  ### Usage in Code                                                             
  ```tsx

  invoiceType: 'credit_addon'

  itemDescription: 'Therapy Session'                                            
  ```

  shows a faint gauge skeleton + "Pending ¬∑ OWI weighting sign-off" ‚ÄĒ because
  OWI is pending sign-off, not k-suppressed. Same honest treatment for % High 
  Stress ("needs PSS-10") and Therapy Utilization ("needs session-booking
  data").

  So every card now has a meaningful visual ‚ÄĒ a number, a bar, a gauge, or a
  clear "what unlocks this" state ‚ÄĒ and nothing reads as purple. The boxes that
  are genuinely empty (because OWI is gated / instruments aren't in the battery
  / cohorts are sub-5) now explain why and preview what will appear, rather than
  sitting blank.
